                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.util;

import com.rabbitmq.client.Channel;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Connection;
import com.rabbitmq.client.ConnectionFactory;

public class RabbitConnectUtil {
    public static Channel getChannel() throws Exception {
        ConnectionFactory factory = new ConnectionFactory();
        factory.setHost("192.168.100.100");
        factory.setUsername("admin");
        factory.setPassword("admin");
        Connection connection = factory.newConnection();
        return connection.createChannel();
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.demo;

import com.example.rabbitmq.util.RabbitConnectUtil;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Channel;

public class Producer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "demo";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        /**
         * ç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªé˜Ÿåˆ—
         * 1. é˜Ÿåˆ—åç§°
         * 2. é˜Ÿåˆ—é‡Œé¢çš„æ¶ˆæ¯æ˜¯å¦æŒä¹…åŒ–ï¼Œé»˜è®¤æ¶ˆæ¯å­˜å‚¨åœ¨å†…å­˜ä¸­
         * 3. è¯¥é˜Ÿåˆ—æ˜¯å¦åªä¾›ä¸€ä¸ªæ¶ˆè´¹è€…è¿›è¡Œæ¶ˆè´¹ï¼Œæ˜¯å¦è¿›è¡Œå…±äº«ï¼Œé»˜è®¤trueï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¤šä¸ªæ¶ˆè´¹è€…æ¶ˆè´¹
         * 4. æ˜¯å¦è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ é™¤ï¼šæœ€åä¸€ä¸ªæ¶ˆè´¹è€…ç«¯å¼€è¿æ¥ä»¥åï¼Œè¯¥é˜Ÿåˆ—æ˜¯å¦è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ é™¤ï¼Œtrueï¼šè‡ªåŠ¨åˆ é™¤
         * 5. å…¶ä»–å‚æ•°
         */
        channel.queueDeclare(QUEUE_NAME, false, false, false, null);
        String message = "Hello RabbitMQ";
        /**
         * å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯
         * 1. å‘é€åˆ°é‚£ä¸ªäº¤æ¢æœº
         * 2. è·¯ç”±çš„ key
         * 3. å…¶ä»–çš„å‚æ•°ä¿¡æ¯
         * 4. å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯çš„æ¶ˆæ¯ä½“
         */
        channel.basicPublish("", QUEUE_NAME, null, message.getBytes());
        System.out.println("æ¶ˆæ¯å‘é€å®Œæ¯•...");
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.demo;

import com.example.rabbitmq.util.RabbitConnectUtil;
import com.rabbitmq.client.CancelCallback;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Channel;
import com.rabbitmq.client.DeliverCallback;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Delivery;

import java.io.IOException;

public class Consumer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "demo";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        /**
         * æ¶ˆè´¹è€…æ¶ˆè´¹æ¶ˆæ¯
         * 1.æ¶ˆè´¹å“ªä¸ªé˜Ÿåˆ—
         * 2.æ¶ˆè´¹æˆåŠŸä¹‹åæ˜¯å¦è¦è‡ªåŠ¨åº”ç­” true ä»£è¡¨è‡ªåŠ¨åº”ç­” false æ‰‹åŠ¨åº”ç­”
         * 3.æ¶ˆè´¹è€…æ¶ˆè´¹æ¶ˆæ¯çš„å›è°ƒ
         * 4.å–æ¶ˆæ¶ˆè´¹çš„å›è°ƒæ¥å£ï¼Œå¦‚æ¶ˆè´¹çš„æ—¶å€™é˜Ÿåˆ—è¢«åˆ é™¤æ‰
         */
        channel.basicConsume(
                QUEUE_NAME,
                true,
                // æ¨é€çš„æ¶ˆæ¯è¿›è¡Œæ¶ˆè´¹çš„å›è°ƒ
                new DeliverCallback() {
                    @Override
                    public void handle(String s, Delivery delivery) throws IOException {
                        System.out.println(new String(delivery.getBody()));
                    }
                },
                // å–æ¶ˆæ¶ˆè´¹çš„å›è°ƒ
                new CancelCallback() {
                    @Override
                    public void handle(String s) throws IOException {
                        System.out.println("æ¶ˆæ¯æ¶ˆè´¹è¢«ä¸­æ–­");
                    }
                });
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      # Work Queues

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ å·¥ä½œé˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼ˆåˆç§°ä»»åŠ¡é˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼‰ä¸»è¦æ€æƒ³ï¼šé¿å…ç«‹å³æ‰§è¡Œèµ„æºå¯†é›†å‹ä»»åŠ¡ï¼Œè€Œä¸å¾—ä¸ç­‰å¾…å®ƒå®Œæˆã€‚ ç›¸åæˆ‘ä»¬å®‰æ’ä»»åŠ¡åœ¨ä¹‹åæ‰§è¡Œã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬æŠŠä»»åŠ¡å°è£…ä¸ºæ¶ˆæ¯å¹¶å°†å…¶å‘é€åˆ°é˜Ÿåˆ—ã€‚åœ¨åå°è¿è¡Œçš„å·¥ä½œè¿› ç¨‹å°†å¼¹å‡ºä»»åŠ¡å¹¶æœ€ç»ˆæ‰§è¡Œä½œä¸šã€‚å½“æœ‰å¤šä¸ªå·¥ä½œçº¿ç¨‹æ—¶ï¼Œè¿™äº›å·¥ä½œçº¿ç¨‹å°†ä¸€èµ·å¤„ç†è¿™äº›ä»»åŠ¡ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      ä¸€ä¸ªæ¶ˆæ¯åªèƒ½è¢«å¤„ç†ä¸€æ¬¡ï¼Œé€šè¿‡è½®è¯¢çš„å½¢å¼æ‰§è¡Œå·¥ä½œé˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸­çš„ä»»åŠ¡ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      è½®è®­åˆ†å‘æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      å…ˆå¯åŠ¨ä¸¤ä¸ªæ¶ˆè´¹è€…ï¼Œå†å¯åŠ¨ä¸€ä¸ªç”Ÿäº§è€…ï¼Œä¼šå‘ç°å¯¹äºç”Ÿäº§çš„æ¶ˆæ¯ä¼šè½®è¯¢ä¾æ¬¡è¿›è¡Œæ¶ˆè´¹ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      ç”Ÿäº§è€…ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.workqueue;

import com.example.rabbitmq.util.RabbitConnectUtil;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Channel;

import java.util.Scanner;

public class Producer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "workqueue";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.queueDeclare(QUEUE_NAME, false, false, false, null);
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        while (sc.hasNext()) {
            String message = sc.nextLine();
            channel.basicPublish("", QUEUE_NAME, null, message.getBytes());
            System.out.println("æ¶ˆæ¯å‘é€å®Œæˆï¼š" + message);
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      æ¶ˆè´¹è€…ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.workqueue;

import com.example.rabbitmq.util.RabbitConnectUtil;
import com.rabbitmq.client.CancelCallback;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Channel;
import com.rabbitmq.client.DeliverCallback;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Delivery;

import java.io.IOException;

public class Consumer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "workqueue";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        System.out.println("ç­‰å¾…æ¥å—æ¶ˆæ¯...");
        channel.basicConsume(QUEUE_NAME, true,
                new DeliverCallback() {
                    @Override
                    public void handle(String s, Delivery delivery) throws IOException {
                        System.out.println("Consumer æ”¶åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼š" + 
                                           new String(delivery.getBody()));
                    }
                },
                new CancelCallback() {
                    @Override
                    public void handle(String s) throws IOException {
                        System.out.println(s + "æ¶ˆè´¹è€…å–æ¶ˆæ¶ˆè´¹æ¥å£å›è°ƒé€»è¾‘");
                    }
                }
        );
        System.out.println("Consumer01 ç­‰å¾…...");
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      ç”Ÿäº§è€…ä¾æ¬¡å‘é€ï¼šA B C D

                                                                                                                                          /**
     * Acknowledge one or several received
     * messages. Supply the deliveryTag from the {@link com.rabbitmq.client.AMQP.Basic.GetOk}
     * or {@link com.rabbitmq.client.AMQP.Basic.Deliver} method
     * containing the received message being acknowledged.
     * @see com.rabbitmq.client.AMQP.Basic.Ack
     * @param deliveryTag the tag from the received {@link com.rabbitmq.client.AMQP.Basic.GetOk} or {@link com.rabbitmq.client.AMQP.Basic.Deliver}
     * @param multiple true to acknowledge all messages up to and
     * including the supplied delivery tag; false to acknowledge just
     * the supplied delivery tag.
     * @throws java.io.IOException if an error is encountered
     */
    void basicAck(long deliveryTag, boolean multiple) throws IOException;

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.ack;

import com.example.rabbitmq.util.RabbitConnectUtil;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Channel;

import java.util.Scanner;

public class Producer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "ack_queue";
	
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.queueDeclare(QUEUE_NAME, false, false, false, null);
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        while (sc.hasNext()) {
            String message = sc.nextLine();
            channel.basicPublish("", QUEUE_NAME, null, message.getBytes());
            System.out.println("æ¶ˆæ¯å‘é€å®Œæˆï¼š" + message);
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.ack;

import com.example.rabbitmq.util.RabbitConnectUtil;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Channel;
import com.rabbitmq.client.DeliverCallback;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Delivery;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

/**
 * æµ‹è¯•æ¶ˆæ¯åº”ç­”
 */
public class Consumer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "ack_queue";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        System.out.println("Consumer01ç­‰å¾…æ¥å—æ¶ˆæ¯...");
        DeliverCallback deliverCallback = new DeliverCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s, Delivery delivery) throws IOException {
                System.out.println(s); // amq.ctag-Gi369GilFESPvGyykhK3pg
                try {
                    TimeUnit.SECONDS.sleep(2);
                    System.out.println("Consumerï¼š" + new String(delivery.getBody()));
                } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                    e.printStackTrace();
                }
                // å‚æ•°ä¸€ï¼šæ¶ˆæ¯æ ‡è®°ï¼Œå‚æ•°äºŒï¼šæ˜¯å¦æ‰¹é‡åº”ç­”
                channel.basicAck(delivery.getEnvelope().getDeliveryTag(), false);
            }
        };
        // æ‰‹åŠ¨åº”ç­”

        channel.basicConsume(QUEUE_NAME, autoAck, deliverCallback, (consumerTag) -> {
            System.out.println("æ¶ˆè´¹è€…å–æ¶ˆæ¶ˆè´¹æ¥å£å›è°ƒé€»è¾‘");
        });
    }

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.durable;

import com.example.rabbitmq.util.RabbitConnectUtil;
import com.rabbitmq.client.Channel;
import com.rabbitmq.client.MessageProperties;

import java.util.Scanner;

public class Producer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "durable_queue";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        // è®¾ç½®é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸ºæŒä¹…åŒ–
        boolean durable = true;
        channel.queueDeclare(QUEUE_NAME, durable, false, false, null);
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        while (sc.hasNext()) {
            String message = sc.nextLine();
            // channel.basicPublish("", QUEUE_NAME, null, message.getBytes());
            // è®¾ç½®æ¶ˆæ¯ä¸ºæŒä¹…åŒ–
            channel.basicPublish("", QUEUE_NAME, MessageProperties.PERSISTENT_TEXT_PLAIN, message.getBytes());
            System.out.println("æ¶ˆæ¯å‘é€å®Œæˆï¼š" + message);
        }
    }
}

    boolean autoAck = false;
    channel.basicConsume(QUEUE_NAME, autoAck, deliverCallback, cancleCallBack});

                                                                                                                                      public class Producer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "durable_queue";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        // è®¾ç½®é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸ºæŒä¹…åŒ–
        boolean durable = true;
        channel.queueDeclare(QUEUE_NAME, durable, false, false, null);
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        while (sc.hasNext()) {
            String message = sc.nextLine();
            // channel.basicPublish("", QUEUE_NAME, null, message.getBytes());
            channel.basicPublish("", QUEUE_NAME, MessageProperties.PERSISTENT_TEXT_PLAIN, message.getBytes());
            System.out.println("æ¶ˆæ¯å‘é€å®Œæˆï¼š" + message);
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      public class Consumer {

                System.out.println(s); // amq.ctag-Gi369GilFESPvGyykhK3pg

                    e.printStackTrace();
                }
                // å‚æ•°ä¸€ï¼šæ¶ˆæ¯æ ‡è®°ï¼Œå‚æ•°äºŒï¼šæ˜¯å¦æ‰¹é‡åº”ç­”
                channel.basicAck(delivery.getEnvelope().getDeliveryTag(), false);

        };

         * è®¾ç½®Qos=0ï¼šæ ‡è¯†è½®è¯¢
         * è®¾ç½®Qos=1ï¼šè¡¨ç¤ºä¸å…¬å¹³åˆ†å‘

            System.out.println("æ¶ˆè´¹è€…å–æ¶ˆæ¶ˆè´¹æ¥å£å›è°ƒé€»è¾‘");
        });
    }

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ è¿™æ˜¯ä¸€ç§ç®€å•çš„ç¡®è®¤æ–¹å¼ï¼Œå®ƒæ˜¯ä¸€ç§åŒæ­¥ç¡®è®¤å‘å¸ƒçš„æ–¹å¼ï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯å‘å¸ƒä¸€ä¸ªæ¶ˆæ¯ä¹‹ååªæœ‰å®ƒè¢«ç¡®è®¤å‘å¸ƒï¼Œåç»­çš„æ¶ˆæ¯æ‰èƒ½ç»§ç»­å‘å¸ƒï¼ŒwaitForConfirmsOrDie(long) è¿™ä¸ªæ–¹æ³•åªæœ‰åœ¨æ¶ˆæ¯è¢«ç¡®è®¤çš„æ—¶å€™æ‰è¿”å›ï¼Œå¦‚æœåœ¨æŒ‡å®šæ—¶é—´èŒƒå›´å†…è¿™ä¸ªæ¶ˆæ¯æ²¡æœ‰è¢«ç¡®è®¤é‚£ä¹ˆå®ƒå°†æŠ›å‡ºå¼‚å¸¸ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ è¿™ç§ç¡®è®¤æ–¹å¼æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªæœ€å¤§çš„ç¼ºç‚¹å°±æ˜¯ï¼šå‘å¸ƒé€Ÿåº¦ç‰¹åˆ«çš„æ…¢ï¼Œå¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰ç¡®è®¤å‘å¸ƒçš„æ¶ˆæ¯å°±ä¼šé˜»å¡æ‰€æœ‰åç»­æ¶ˆæ¯çš„å‘å¸ƒï¼Œè¿™ç§æ–¹å¼æœ€å¤šæä¾›æ¯ç§’ä¸è¶…è¿‡æ•°ç™¾æ¡å‘å¸ƒæ¶ˆæ¯çš„ååé‡ã€‚å½“ç„¶å¯¹äºæŸäº›åº”ç”¨ç¨‹åºæ¥è¯´è¿™å¯èƒ½å·²ç»è¶³å¤Ÿäº†ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      private static final int MESSAGE_COUNT = 1000;
private static final String queue_name = "confirm_queue";
/**
 * å•ä¸ªæ¶ˆæ¯å‘å¸ƒ
 */
public static void singleMessagePublish() throws Exception {
    Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
    // è®¾ç½®é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸ºæŒä¹…åŒ–
    boolean durable = true;
    channel.queueDeclare(queue_name, durable, false, false, null);
    // å¼€å¯ç¡®è®¤å‘å¸ƒ
    channel.confirmSelect();
    long start = System.currentTimeMillis();
    for (int i = 0; i < MESSAGE_COUNT; i++) {
        channel.basicPublish("", queue_name, null, String.valueOf(i).getBytes());
        boolean ret = channel.waitForConfirms();
        //æœåŠ¡ç«¯è¿”å› false æˆ–è¶…æ—¶æ—¶é—´å†…æœªè¿”å›ï¼Œç”Ÿäº§è€…å¯ä»¥æ¶ˆæ¯é‡å‘
        if (ret) {
            System.out.println("æ¶ˆæ¯å‘é€æˆåŠŸ");
        }
    }
    long end = System.currentTimeMillis();
    System.out.println("å‘å¸ƒ" + MESSAGE_COUNT + "ä¸ªå•ç‹¬ç¡®è®¤æ¶ˆæ¯,è€—æ—¶" + (end - start) + "ms");
}

                                                                                                                                      # æ‰¹é‡ç¡®è®¤å‘å¸ƒ

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ ä¸Šé¢é‚£ç§æ–¹å¼éå¸¸æ…¢ï¼Œä¸å•ä¸ªç­‰å¾…ç¡®è®¤æ¶ˆæ¯ç›¸æ¯”ï¼Œå…ˆå‘å¸ƒä¸€æ‰¹æ¶ˆæ¯ç„¶åä¸€èµ·ç¡®è®¤å¯ä»¥æå¤§åœ°æé«˜ååé‡ï¼Œå½“ç„¶è¿™ç§æ–¹å¼çš„ç¼ºç‚¹æ˜¯ï¼šå½“å‘ç”Ÿæ•…éšœå¯¼è‡´å‘å¸ƒå‡ºç°é—®é¢˜æ—¶ï¼Œä¸çŸ¥é“æ˜¯å“ªä¸ªæ¶ˆæ¯å‡ºç°é—®é¢˜äº†ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¿…é¡»å°†æ•´ä¸ªæ‰¹å¤„ç†ä¿å­˜åœ¨å†…å­˜ä¸­ï¼Œä»¥è®°å½•é‡è¦çš„ä¿¡æ¯è€Œåé‡æ–°å‘å¸ƒæ¶ˆæ¯ã€‚å½“ç„¶è¿™ç§æ–¹æ¡ˆä»ç„¶æ˜¯åŒæ­¥çš„ï¼Œä¹Ÿä¸€æ ·é˜»å¡æ¶ˆæ¯çš„å‘å¸ƒã€‚

                                                                                                                                      private static final int MESSAGE_COUNT = 1000;
private static final String queue_name = "confirm_queue";
/**
 * æ‰¹é‡æ¶ˆæ¯å‘å¸ƒ
 */
public static void batchMessagePublish() throws Exception {
    Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
    channel.confirmSelect();
    channel.queueDeclare(queue_name, true, false, false, null);
    long start = System.currentTimeMillis();
    for (int i = 0; i < MESSAGE_COUNT; i++) {
        channel.basicPublish("", queue_name, null, String.valueOf(i).getBytes());
        // æ¯100ä¸ªæ¶ˆæ¯æ‰¹é‡ç¡®è®¤ä¸€æ¬¡
        if (i % 100 == 0) {
            channel.waitForConfirms();
        }
    }
    long end = System.currentTimeMillis();
    System.out.println("å‘å¸ƒ" + MESSAGE_COUNT + "ä¸ªå•æ‰¹é‡ç¡®è®¤æ¶ˆæ¯,è€—æ—¶" + (end - start) + "ms");
}

                                                                                                                                      # å¼‚æ­¥ç¡®è®¤å‘å¸ƒ

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ å¼‚æ­¥ç¡®è®¤è™½ç„¶ç¼–ç¨‹é€»è¾‘æ¯”ä¸Šä¸¤ä¸ªè¦å¤æ‚ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯æ€§ä»·æ¯”æœ€é«˜ï¼Œæ— è®ºæ˜¯å¯é æ€§è¿˜æ˜¯æ•ˆç‡éƒ½æ²¡å¾—è¯´ï¼Œ å®ƒæ˜¯åˆ©ç”¨å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°æ¥è¾¾åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯å¯é æ€§ä¼ é€’çš„ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªä¸­é—´ä»¶ä¹Ÿæ˜¯é€šè¿‡å‡½æ•°å›è°ƒæ¥ä¿è¯æ˜¯å¦æŠ•é€’æˆåŠŸï¼Œ ä¸‹é¢å°±è®©æˆ‘ä»¬æ¥è¯¦ç»†è®²è§£å¼‚æ­¥ç¡®è®¤æ˜¯æ€ä¹ˆå®ç°çš„ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      private static final int MESSAGE_COUNT = 1000;
private static final String queue_name = "confirm_queue";
/**
 * å¼‚æ­¥æ¶ˆæ¯å‘å¸ƒ
 */
public static void asyncPublishMessage() throws Exception {
    Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
    channel.queueDeclare(queue_name, false, false, false, null);
    channel.confirmSelect();
    // å­˜æ”¾æ¶ˆæ¯ç¼–å·ä¸å…·ä½“ä¿¡æ¯
    ConcurrentSkipListMap<Long, String> outstandingConfirms = new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>();
    /**
     * ç¡®è®¤æ”¶åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯çš„ä¸€ä¸ªå›è°ƒ
     * å‚æ•°ä¸€ï¼šæ¶ˆæ¯åºåˆ—å·
     * å‚æ•°äºŒï¼štrue ï¼ˆæ‰¹é‡åˆ é™¤ï¼‰å¯ä»¥ç¡®è®¤å°äºç­‰äºå½“å‰åºåˆ—å·çš„æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼Œfalse ç¡®è®¤å½“å‰åºåˆ—å·æ¶ˆæ¯
     */
    ConfirmCallback confirmCallback = new ConfirmCallback() {
        @Override
        public void handle(long sequenceNumber, boolean multiple) throws IOException {
            // æ‰¹é‡åˆ é™¤
            if (multiple) {
                //è¿”å›çš„æ˜¯å°äºç­‰äºå½“å‰åºåˆ—å·çš„æœªç¡®è®¤æ¶ˆæ¯ æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ª map
                ConcurrentNavigableMap<Long, String> confirmed =
                    outstandingConfirms.headMap(sequenceNumber, true);
                //æ¸…é™¤è¯¥éƒ¨åˆ†æœªç¡®è®¤æ¶ˆæ¯(æ‰¹é‡æ¸…é™¤)
                confirmed.clear();
            } else {
                //åªæ¸…é™¤å½“å‰åºåˆ—å·çš„æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼ˆå•ä¸ªåˆ é™¤ï¼‰
                outstandingConfirms.remove(sequenceNumber);
            }
        }
    };
    ConfirmCallback nackCallback = (sequenceNumber, multiple) -> {
        String message = outstandingConfirms.get(sequenceNumber);
        System.out.println("å‘å¸ƒçš„æ¶ˆæ¯" + message + "æœªè¢«ç¡®è®¤ï¼Œåºåˆ—å·" + sequenceNumber);
    };
    /**
     * æ·»åŠ ä¸€ä¸ªå¼‚æ­¥ç¡®è®¤çš„ç›‘å¬å™¨
     * 1.ç¡®è®¤æ”¶åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯çš„å›è°ƒ
     * 2.æœªæ”¶åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯çš„å›è°ƒ
     */
    channel.addConfirmListener(confirmCallback, nackCallback);
    long begin = System.currentTimeMillis();
    for (int i = 0; i < MESSAGE_COUNT; i++) {
        String message = "æ¶ˆæ¯" + i;
        /**
         * channel.getNextPublishSeqNo()è·å–ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªæ¶ˆæ¯çš„åºåˆ—å·
         * é€šè¿‡åºåˆ—å·ä¸æ¶ˆæ¯ä½“è¿›è¡Œä¸€ä¸ªå…³è”
         * å…¨éƒ¨éƒ½æ˜¯æœªç¡®è®¤çš„æ¶ˆæ¯ä½“
         */
        outstandingConfirms.put(channel.getNextPublishSeqNo(), message);
        channel.basicPublish("", queue_name, null, message.getBytes());
    }
    long end = System.currentTimeMillis();
    System.out.println("å‘å¸ƒ" + MESSAGE_COUNT + "ä¸ªå¼‚æ­¥ç¡®è®¤æ¶ˆæ¯,è€—æ—¶" + (end - begin) + "ms");
}

                                                                                                                                      public enum BuiltinExchangeType {

    DIRECT("direct"), FANOUT("fanout"), TOPIC("topic"), HEADERS("headers");

    private final String type;

    BuiltinExchangeType(String type) {
        this.type = type;
    }

    public String getType() {
        return type;
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      # Fanout

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ Fanout æ˜¯å°†æ¥æ”¶åˆ°çš„æ‰€æœ‰æ¶ˆæ¯å¹¿æ’­åˆ°å®ƒçŸ¥é“çš„æ‰€æœ‰é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸­ï¼Œç­‰åŒäºä¸Šè¿°çš„å‘å¸ƒè®¢é˜…æ¨¡å¼ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ ç”Ÿäº§è€…å‘é€æ—¥å¿—ä¿¡æ¯åˆ° broker ä¸Šé¢ï¼Œæ¶ˆè´¹è€…ä¸€å°†ä¿¡æ¯æ˜¾ç¤ºåˆ°æ§åˆ¶å°ä¸Šï¼Œæ¶ˆè´¹è€…äºŒå°†æ—¥å¿—ä¿¡æ¯å­˜å…¥ç£ç›˜ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      ReceiveLogs01 å°†æ¥æ”¶åˆ°çš„æ¶ˆæ¯æ‰“å°åœ¨æ§åˆ¶å°ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * æµ‹è¯•äº¤æ¢æœºç±»å‹
 * å°†æ¥æ”¶åˆ°çš„æ¶ˆæ¯æ‰“å°åˆ°æ§åˆ¶å°
 */
public class ReceiveLogs01 {
    private static final String EXCHANGE_NAME = "logs";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.exchangeDeclare(EXCHANGE_NAME, BuiltinExchangeType.FANOUT);
        /**
         * ç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªéšæœºé˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼šå½“æ¶ˆè´¹è€…æ–­å¼€å’Œè¯¥é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„è¿æ¥æ—¶é˜Ÿåˆ—è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ é™¤
         */
        String queueName = channel.queueDeclare().getQueue();
        // ç»‘å®šé˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸äº¤æ¢æœºï¼Œå…¶ä¸­routingkey(ä¹Ÿç§°ä¹‹ä¸º binding key)è®¾ç½®ä¸ºç©ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        channel.queueBind(queueName, EXCHANGE_NAME, "");
        System.out.println("ReceiveLogs01ç­‰å¾…æ¥å—æ¶ˆæ¯...");
        DeliverCallback deliverCallback = new DeliverCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s, Delivery delivery) throws IOException {
                System.out.println("æ§åˆ¶å°æ‰“å°æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼š" + new String(delivery.getBody()));
            }
        };
        CancelCallback cancelCallback = new CancelCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s) throws IOException {
            }
        };
        channel.basicConsume(queueName, true, deliverCallback, cancelCallback);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      ReceiveLogs02 å°†æ¥æ”¶åˆ°çš„æ¶ˆæ¯å­˜å‚¨åœ¨ç£ç›˜ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * æµ‹è¯•äº¤æ¢æœºç±»å‹
 * å°†æ¥æ”¶åˆ°çš„æ¶ˆæ¯å†™å…¥æ–‡ä»¶
 */
public class ReceiveLogs02 {
    private static final String EXCHANGE_NAME = "logs";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.exchangeDeclare(EXCHANGE_NAME, BuiltinExchangeType.FANOUT);
        /**
         * ç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªéšæœºé˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼šå½“æ¶ˆè´¹è€…æ–­å¼€å’Œè¯¥é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„è¿æ¥æ—¶é˜Ÿåˆ—è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ é™¤
         */
        String queueName = channel.queueDeclare().getQueue();
        // ç»‘å®šé˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸äº¤æ¢æœºï¼Œå…¶ä¸­routingkey(ä¹Ÿç§°ä¹‹ä¸º binding key)è®¾ç½®ä¸ºç©ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        channel.queueBind(queueName, EXCHANGE_NAME, "");
        System.out.println("ReceiveLogs02ç­‰å¾…æ¥å—æ¶ˆæ¯...");
        DeliverCallback deliverCallback = new DeliverCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s, Delivery delivery) throws IOException {
                String message = new String(delivery.getBody());
                FileUtils.writeStringToFile(new File("rabbit.txt"), message);
                System.out.println("æ•°æ®å†™å…¥æ–‡ä»¶æˆåŠŸ");
            }
        };
        CancelCallback cancelCallback = new CancelCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s) throws IOException {
            }
        };
        channel.basicConsume(queueName, true, deliverCallback, cancelCallback);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      EmitLog å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯ç»™ä¸¤ä¸ªæ¶ˆè´¹è€…æ¥æ”¶ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * äº¤æ¢æœºæµ‹è¯•ï¼š
 * æäº¤æ—¥å¿—
 */
public class EmitLog {
    private static final String EXCHANGE_NAME = "logs";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.exchangeDeclare(EXCHANGE_NAME, BuiltinExchangeType.FANOUT);
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        while (sc.hasNext()) {
            String message = sc.nextLine();
            channel.basicPublish(EXCHANGE_NAME, "", null, message.getBytes());
            System.out.println("æ¶ˆæ¯å‘é€å®Œæˆï¼š" + message);
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      # Direct exchange

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ ä¸Šé¢å¯ä»¥å‘è®¸å¤šæ¥æ”¶è€…å¹¿æ’­æ—¥å¿—æ¶ˆæ¯ã€‚ä½†å¦‚ä½•åªè®©æŸä¸ªæ¶ˆè´¹è€…è®¢é˜…å‘å¸ƒçš„éƒ¨åˆ†æ¶ˆæ¯ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚åªæŠŠä¸¥é‡é”™è¯¯æ¶ˆæ¯å®šå‘å­˜å‚¨åˆ°æ—¥å¿—æ–‡ä»¶ï¼ŒåŒæ—¶ä»ç„¶èƒ½å¤Ÿåœ¨æ§åˆ¶å°ä¸Šæ‰“å°æ‰€æœ‰æ—¥å¿—æ¶ˆæ¯ã€‚å¯¹äº bindingsï¼Œé˜Ÿåˆ—åªå¯¹å®ƒç»‘å®šçš„äº¤æ¢æœºçš„æ¶ˆæ¯æ„Ÿå…´è¶£ï¼Œæœ‰æ¡ä»¶çš„å¹¿æ’­æ¶ˆæ¯ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      channel.queueBind(queueName, EXCHANGE_NAME, "routingKey");

                                                                                                                                      Direct exchange ä»‹ç»ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ å¸Œæœ›å°†æ—¥å¿—æ¶ˆæ¯å†™å…¥ç£ç›˜çš„ç¨‹åºä»…æ¥æ”¶ä¸¥é‡é”™è¯¯ï¼ˆerrrosï¼‰ï¼Œè€Œä¸å­˜å‚¨å“ªäº›è­¦å‘Šï¼ˆwarningï¼‰æˆ–ä¿¡æ¯ï¼ˆinfoï¼‰æ—¥å¿—æ¶ˆæ¯é¿å…æµªè´¹ç£ç›˜ç©ºé—´ã€‚Fanout è¿™ç§äº¤æ¢ç±»å‹å¹¶ä¸èƒ½ç»™æˆ‘ä»¬å¸¦æ¥å¾ˆå¤§çš„çµæ´»æ€§ï¼Œå®ƒåªèƒ½è¿›è¡Œæ— æ„è¯†çš„å¹¿æ’­ï¼Œåœ¨è¿™é‡Œæˆ‘ä»¬å°†ä½¿ç”¨ direct è¿™ç§ç±»å‹æ¥è¿›è¡Œæ›¿æ¢ï¼Œè¿™ç§ç±»å‹çš„å·¥ä½œæ–¹å¼æ˜¯ï¼Œæ¶ˆæ¯åªå»åˆ°å®ƒç»‘å®šçš„ routingKey é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸­å»ã€‚

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ åœ¨ä¸Šé¢è¿™å¼ å›¾ä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥çœ‹åˆ° X ç»‘å®šäº†ä¸¤ä¸ªé˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼Œç»‘å®šç±»å‹æ˜¯ directã€‚é˜Ÿåˆ— Q1 ç»‘å®šé”®ä¸º orangeï¼Œ é˜Ÿåˆ— Q2 ç»‘å®šé”®æœ‰ä¸¤ä¸ªï¼šä¸€ä¸ªç»‘å®šé”®ä¸º blackï¼Œå¦ä¸€ä¸ªç»‘å®šé”®ä¸º greenã€‚åœ¨è¿™ç§ç»‘å®šæƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œç”Ÿäº§è€…å‘å¸ƒæ¶ˆæ¯åˆ° exchange ä¸Šï¼Œç»‘å®šé”®ä¸º orange çš„æ¶ˆæ¯ä¼šè¢«å‘å¸ƒåˆ°é˜Ÿåˆ— Q1ã€‚ç»‘å®šé”®ä¸º black å’Œ greençš„æ¶ˆæ¯ä¼šè¢«å‘å¸ƒåˆ°é˜Ÿåˆ— Q2ï¼Œå…¶ä»–æ¶ˆæ¯ç±»å‹çš„æ¶ˆæ¯å°†è¢«ä¸¢å¼ƒã€‚

                                                                                                                                      å¤šé‡ç»‘å®šï¼š

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ å¦‚æœ exchange çš„ç»‘å®šç±»å‹æ˜¯ directï¼Œä½†æ˜¯å®ƒç»‘å®šçš„å¤šä¸ªé˜Ÿåˆ—çš„ key å¦‚æœéƒ½ç›¸åŒï¼Œåœ¨è¿™ç§æƒ…å†µä¸‹è™½ç„¶ç»‘å®šç±»å‹æ˜¯ direct ä½†æ˜¯å®ƒè¡¨ç°çš„å°±å’Œ fanout æœ‰ç‚¹ç±»ä¼¼äº†ï¼Œå°±è·Ÿå¹¿æ’­å·®ä¸å¤šã€‚

                                                                                                                                      ç¤ºä¾‹

                                                                                                                                      ReceiveLogsDirect01ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * äº¤æ¢æœºç±»å‹ï¼šdirect
 * æ¥æ”¶errorç±»å‹
 */
public class ReceiveLogsDirect01 {
    private static final String EXCHANGE_NAME = "direct_logs";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.exchangeDeclare(EXCHANGE_NAME, BuiltinExchangeType.DIRECT);
        String queueName = "disk";
        channel.queueDeclare(queueName, false, false, false, null);
        channel.queueBind(queueName, EXCHANGE_NAME, "error");
        System.out.println("ç­‰å¾…æ¥æ”¶æ¶ˆæ¯...");
        DeliverCallback deliverCallback = new DeliverCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s, Delivery delivery) throws IOException {
                String message = "routingKey: " + delivery.getEnvelope().getRoutingKey() + " : " + "æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼š" + delivery.getEnvelope();
                FileUtils.writeStringToFile(new File("rabbit.txt"), message);
                System.out.println("é”™è¯¯æ—¥å¿—å·²ç»æ¥æ”¶...");
            }
        };
        CancelCallback cancelCallback = new CancelCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s) throws IOException {
            }
        };
        channel.basicConsume(queueName, true, deliverCallback, cancelCallback);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      ReceiveLogsDirect02ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * äº¤æ¢æœºç±»å‹ï¼šdirect
 * æ¥æ”¶infoï¼Œwarnç±»å‹
 */
public class ReceiveLogsDirect02 {
    private static final String EXCHANGE_NAME = "direct_logs";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.exchangeDeclare(EXCHANGE_NAME, BuiltinExchangeType.DIRECT);
        String queueName = "console";
        channel.queueDeclare(queueName, false, false, false, null);
        channel.queueBind(queueName, EXCHANGE_NAME, "info");
        channel.queueBind(queueName, EXCHANGE_NAME, "warn");
        System.out.println("ç­‰å¾…æ¥æ”¶æ¶ˆæ¯...");
        DeliverCallback deliverCallback = new DeliverCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s, Delivery delivery) throws IOException {
                String message = "routingKey: " + delivery.getEnvelope().getRoutingKey() + " : " + "æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼š" + new String(delivery.getBody());
                System.out.println(message);
            }
        };
        CancelCallback cancelCallback = new CancelCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s) throws IOException {
            }
        };
        channel.basicConsume(queueName, true, deliverCallback, cancelCallback);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      EmitLogDirectï¼š

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * äº¤æ¢æœºç±»å‹ï¼šdirect
 */
public class EmitLogDirect {
    private static final String EXCHANGE_NAME = "direct_logs";
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.exchangeDeclare(EXCHANGE_NAME, BuiltinExchangeType.DIRECT);
        Map<String, String> dataBindingMap = new HashMap<>();
        dataBindingMap.put("info", "info_message");
        dataBindingMap.put("error", "error_message");
        dataBindingMap.put("warn", "warn_message");
        dataBindingMap.put("debug", "debug_message");
        for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : dataBindingMap.entrySet()) {
            channel.basicPublish(EXCHANGE_NAME, entry.getKey(), null, 
                                 entry.getValue().getBytes());
            System.out.println("ç”Ÿäº§è€…å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼š" + entry.getValue());
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * æµ‹è¯•äº¤æ¢æœº:topic
 */
public class EmitLogTopic {
    private static final String EXCHANGE_NAME = "topic_logs";

    public static void main(String[] argv) throws Exception {
        try (Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel()) {
            channel.exchangeDeclare(EXCHANGE_NAME, "topic");
            Map<String, String> bindingKeyMap = new HashMap<>();
            bindingKeyMap.put("quick.orange.rabbit", "è¢«é˜Ÿåˆ— Q1Q2 æ¥æ”¶åˆ°");
            bindingKeyMap.put("lazy.orange.elephant", "è¢«é˜Ÿåˆ— Q1Q2 æ¥æ”¶åˆ°");
            bindingKeyMap.put("quick.orange.fox", "è¢«é˜Ÿåˆ— Q1 æ¥æ”¶åˆ°");
            bindingKeyMap.put("lazy.brown.fox", "è¢«é˜Ÿåˆ— Q2 æ¥æ”¶åˆ°");
            bindingKeyMap.put("lazy.pink.rabbit", "è™½ç„¶æ»¡è¶³ä¸¤ä¸ªç»‘å®šä½†åªè¢«é˜Ÿåˆ— Q2 æ¥æ”¶ä¸€æ¬¡");
            bindingKeyMap.put("quick.brown.fox", "ä¸åŒ¹é…ä»»ä½•ç»‘å®šä¸ä¼šè¢«ä»»ä½•é˜Ÿåˆ—æ¥æ”¶åˆ°ä¼šè¢«ä¸¢å¼ƒ");
            bindingKeyMap.put("quick.orange.male.rabbit", "æ˜¯å››ä¸ªå•è¯ä¸åŒ¹é…ä»»ä½•ç»‘å®šä¼šè¢«ä¸¢å¼ƒ");
            bindingKeyMap.put("lazy.orange.male.rabbit", "æ˜¯å››ä¸ªå•è¯ä½†åŒ¹é… Q2");
            for (Map.Entry<String, String> bindingKeyEntry : bindingKeyMap.entrySet()) {
                String bindingKey = bindingKeyEntry.getKey();
                String message = bindingKeyEntry.getValue();
                channel.basicPublish(EXCHANGE_NAME, bindingKey, null,
                        message.getBytes("UTF-8"));
                System.out.println("ç”Ÿäº§è€…å‘å‡ºæ¶ˆæ¯ï¼š" + message);
            }
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      public class ReceiveLogsTopic01 {
    private static final String EXCHANGE_NAME = "topic_logs";
    public static void main(String[] argv) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.exchangeDeclare(EXCHANGE_NAME, "topic");
        String queueName = "Q1";
        channel.queueDeclare(queueName, false, false, false, null);
        channel.queueBind(queueName, EXCHANGE_NAME, "*.orange.*");
        System.out.println("ç­‰å¾…æ¥æ”¶æ¶ˆæ¯...");
        DeliverCallback deliverCallback = (consumerTag, delivery) -> {
            String message = new String(delivery.getBody(), "UTF-8");
            System.out.println("æ¥æ”¶é˜Ÿåˆ— :" + queueName + " ç»‘å®šé”®:" + 
                               delivery.getEnvelope().getRoutingKey() + ", æ¶ˆæ¯:" + message);
        };
        channel.basicConsume(queueName, true, deliverCallback, consumerTag -> {});
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * æ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼š
 * TTLè¿‡æœŸ
 */
public class Producer {
    private static final String NORMAL_EXCHANGE = "normal_exchange";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        channel.exchangeDeclare(NORMAL_EXCHANGE, BuiltinExchangeType.DIRECT);
        // è®¾ç½®æ¶ˆæ¯çš„TTLè¿‡æœŸæ—¶é—´:10S
        AMQP.BasicProperties properties = new AMQP.BasicProperties().builder().expiration("10000").build();
        for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
            String message = "info" + i;
            channel.basicPublish(NORMAL_EXCHANGE, "name", properties, message.getBytes());
            System.out.println("ç”Ÿäº§è€…å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼š" + message);
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      æ¶ˆè´¹è€… C1 ä»£ç ï¼ˆå¯åŠ¨ä¹‹åå…³é—­è¯¥æ¶ˆè´¹è€…ï¼Œæ¨¡æ‹Ÿå…¶æ¥æ”¶ä¸åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯ï¼‰

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * æ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼šTTLè¿‡æœŸ
 * å¯åŠ¨ä¹‹åå…³é—­è¯¥æ¶ˆè´¹è€…ï¼Œæ¨¡æ‹Ÿå…¶æ¥æ”¶ä¸åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯
 */
public class Consumer01 {
    private static final String NORMAL_EXCHANGE = "normal_exchange";
    private static final String DEAD_EXCHANGE = "dead_exchange";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        // å£°æ˜æ™®é€šå¯¹åˆ—å’Œæ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—äº¤æ¢æœº
        channel.exchangeDeclare(NORMAL_EXCHANGE, BuiltinExchangeType.DIRECT);
        channel.exchangeDeclare(DEAD_EXCHANGE, BuiltinExchangeType.DIRECT);
        String queueName = "dead-queue";
        channel.queueDeclare(queueName, false, false, false, null);
        // ç»‘å®šæ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—å’Œäº¤æ¢æœº
        channel.queueBind(queueName, DEAD_EXCHANGE, "name02");

        // æ­£å¸¸é˜Ÿåˆ—è®¾ç½®æ­»ä¿¡äº¤æ¢æœº å‚æ•° key æ˜¯å›ºå®šå€¼
        HashMap<String, Object> params = new HashMap<>();
        params.put("x-dead-letter-exchange", DEAD_EXCHANGE);
        params.put("x-dead-letter-routing-key", "name02");

        String normalQueue = "normal-queue";
        channel.queueDeclare(normalQueue, false, false, false, params);
        channel.queueBind(normalQueue, NORMAL_EXCHANGE, "name");
        System.out.println("ç­‰å¾…æ¥æ”¶æ¶ˆæ¯.....");
        DeliverCallback deliverCallback = new DeliverCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s, Delivery delivery) throws IOException {
                System.out.println(new String(delivery.getBody()));
            }
        };
        channel.basicConsume(normalQueue, true, deliverCallback, consumerTag -> {
        });
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      åˆ é™¤åŸå…ˆé˜Ÿåˆ—è¿›è¡Œæµ‹è¯•ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      # æ¶ˆæ¯è¢«æ‹’

                                                                                                                                      ä¿®æ”¹ C1 æ¶ˆè´¹è€…ä»£ç ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      /**
 * æ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼šæ¶ˆæ¯è¢«æ‹’
 * å¯åŠ¨ä¹‹åå…³é—­è¯¥æ¶ˆè´¹è€…ï¼Œæ¨¡æ‹Ÿå…¶æ¥æ”¶ä¸åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯
 */
public class Consumer03 {
    private static final String NORMAL_EXCHANGE = "normal_exchange";
    private static final String DEAD_EXCHANGE = "dead_exchange";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        // å£°æ˜æ™®é€šå¯¹åˆ—å’Œæ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—äº¤æ¢æœº
        channel.exchangeDeclare(NORMAL_EXCHANGE, BuiltinExchangeType.DIRECT);
        channel.exchangeDeclare(DEAD_EXCHANGE, BuiltinExchangeType.DIRECT);
        String queueName = "dead-queue";
        channel.queueDeclare(queueName, false, false, false, null);
        // ç»‘å®šæ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—å’Œäº¤æ¢æœº
        channel.queueBind(queueName, DEAD_EXCHANGE, "name02");

        // æ­£å¸¸é˜Ÿåˆ—è®¾ç½®æ­»ä¿¡äº¤æ¢æœº å‚æ•° key æ˜¯å›ºå®šå€¼
        HashMap<String, Object> params = new HashMap<>();
        params.put("x-dead-letter-exchange", DEAD_EXCHANGE);
        params.put("x-dead-letter-routing-key", "name02");
        // è®¾ç½®æ­£å¸¸é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„é•¿åº¦é™åˆ¶
        params.put("x-max-length", 6);
        String normalQueue = "normal-queue";
        channel.queueDeclare(normalQueue, false, false, false, params);
        channel.queueBind(normalQueue, NORMAL_EXCHANGE, "name");
        System.out.println("ç­‰å¾…æ¥æ”¶æ¶ˆæ¯.....");
        DeliverCallback deliverCallback = new DeliverCallback() {
            @Override
            public void handle(String s, Delivery delivery) throws IOException {
                String message = new String(delivery.getBody());
                if ("info5".equals(message)) {
                    System.out.println("æ¥æ”¶åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯: " + message + " ï¼Œå¹¶æ‹’ç»ç­¾æ”¶è¯¥æ¶ˆæ¯");
                    // requeue è®¾ç½®ä¸º false ä»£è¡¨æ‹’ç»é‡æ–°å…¥é˜Ÿï¼Œè¯¥é˜Ÿåˆ—å¦‚æœé…ç½®äº†æ­»ä¿¡äº¤æ¢æœºå°†å‘é€åˆ°æ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸­
                    channel.basicReject(delivery.getEnvelope().getDeliveryTag(),false);
                }
                // æ‰‹åŠ¨åº”ç­”
                else{
                    System.out.println("æ¥æ”¶åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯: "+message);
                    channel.basicAck(delivery.getEnvelope().getDeliveryTag(), false);
                }
            }
        };
        boolean autoAck = false;
        channel.basicConsume(normalQueue, autoAck, deliverCallback, consumerTag -> {
        });
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      	@Bean("queueA")
    public Queue queueA() {
        Map<String, Object> params = new HashMap<>(3);
        // å£°æ˜å½“å‰é˜Ÿåˆ—ç»‘å®šçš„æ­»ä¿¡äº¤æ¢æœº
        params.put("x-dead-letter-exchange", Y_DEAD_LETTER_EXCHANGE);
        // å£°æ˜å½“å‰é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„æ­»ä¿¡è·¯ç”± key

    }

                                                                                                                                      # é˜Ÿåˆ— TTL

                                                                                                                                      â€‹ åˆ›å»ºä¸¤ä¸ªé˜Ÿåˆ— QA å’Œ QBï¼Œä¸¤è€…é˜Ÿåˆ— TTL åˆ†åˆ«è®¾ç½®ä¸º 10S å’Œ 40Sï¼Œç„¶ååœ¨åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªäº¤æ¢æœº X å’Œæ­»ä¿¡äº¤ æ¢æœº Yï¼Œå®ƒä»¬çš„ç±»å‹éƒ½æ˜¯ directï¼Œåˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªæ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ— QDï¼Œï¼ˆåªåˆ›å»ºç§ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼Œé¿å…è¢«å…¶ä»–é˜Ÿåˆ—æ¶ˆè´¹ï¼‰å®ƒä»¬çš„ç»‘å®šå…³ç³»å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š

                                                                                                                                      é…ç½®ç±»

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.config;

import org.springframework.amqp.core.*;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Qualifier;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

@Configuration
public class TtlQueueConfig {
    public static final String X_EXCHANGE = "X";
    public static final String QUEUE_A = "QA";
    public static final String QUEUE_B = "QB";
    public static final String QUEUE_A_ROUTING_KEY = "XA";
    public static final String QUEUE_B_ROUTING_KEY = "XB";

    public static final String Y_DEAD_LETTER_EXCHANGE = "Y";
    public static final String DEAD_LETTER_QUEUE = "QD";
    public static final String DEAD_LETTER_ROUTING_KEY = "YD";

    @Bean("xExchange")
    public DirectExchange xExchange() {
        return new DirectExchange(X_EXCHANGE);
    }

    @Bean("yExchange")
    public DirectExchange yExchange() {
        return new DirectExchange(Y_DEAD_LETTER_EXCHANGE);
    }

    // å£°æ˜é˜Ÿåˆ— A ttl ä¸º 10s å¹¶ç»‘å®šåˆ°å¯¹åº”çš„æ­»ä¿¡äº¤æ¢æœº
    @Bean("queueA")
    public Queue queueA() {
        Map<String, Object> params = new HashMap<>(3);
        // å£°æ˜å½“å‰é˜Ÿåˆ—ç»‘å®šçš„æ­»ä¿¡äº¤æ¢æœº
        params.put("x-dead-letter-exchange", Y_DEAD_LETTER_EXCHANGE);
        // å£°æ˜å½“å‰é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„æ­»ä¿¡è·¯ç”± key
        params.put("x-dead-letter-routing-key", DEAD_LETTER_ROUTING_KEY);
        // å£°æ˜é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„ TTL
        params.put("x-message-ttl", 10000);
        return QueueBuilder.durable(QUEUE_A).withArguments(params).build();
    }

    // å£°æ˜é˜Ÿåˆ— A ç»‘å®š X äº¤æ¢æœº
    @Bean
    public Binding queueaBindingX(@Qualifier("queueA") Queue queueA,
                                  @Qualifier("xExchange") DirectExchange xExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(queueA).to(xExchange).with("XA");
    }

    // å£°æ˜é˜Ÿåˆ— B ttl ä¸º 40s å¹¶ç»‘å®šåˆ°å¯¹åº”çš„æ­»ä¿¡äº¤æ¢æœº
    @Bean("queueB")
    public Queue queueB() {
        Map<String, Object> args = new HashMap<>(3);
        //å£°æ˜å½“å‰é˜Ÿåˆ—ç»‘å®šçš„æ­»ä¿¡äº¤æ¢æœº
        args.put("x-dead-letter-exchange", Y_DEAD_LETTER_EXCHANGE);
        //å£°æ˜å½“å‰é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„æ­»ä¿¡è·¯ç”± key
        args.put("x-dead-letter-routing-key", "YD");
        //å£°æ˜é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„ TTL
        args.put("x-message-ttl", 40000);
        return QueueBuilder.durable(QUEUE_B).withArguments(args).build();
    }

    // å£°æ˜é˜Ÿåˆ— B ç»‘å®š X äº¤æ¢æœº
    @Bean
    public Binding queuebBindingX(@Qualifier("queueB") Queue queue1B,
                                  @Qualifier("xExchange") DirectExchange xExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(queue1B).to(xExchange).with("XB");
    }

    // å£°æ˜æ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ— QD
    @Bean("queueD")
    public Queue queueD() {
        return new Queue(DEAD_LETTER_QUEUE);
    }

    // å£°æ˜æ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ— QD ç»‘å®šå…³ç³»
    @Bean
    public Binding deadLetterBindingQAD(@Qualifier("queueD") Queue queueD,
                                        @Qualifier("yExchange") DirectExchange yExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(queueD).to(yExchange).with("YD");
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.controller;

import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.amqp.rabbit.core.RabbitTemplate;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PathVariable;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;

import java.util.Date;

@Slf4j
@RequestMapping("ttl")
@RestController
public class SendMsgController {
    @Autowired
    private RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate;

    @GetMapping("/sendMsg/{message}")
    public void sendMsg(@PathVariable String message) {
        log.info("å½“å‰æ—¶é—´ï¼š{},å‘é€ä¸€æ¡ä¿¡æ¯ç»™ä¸¤ä¸ª TTL é˜Ÿåˆ—:{}", new Date(), message);
        rabbitTemplate.convertAndSend("X", "XA", "æ¶ˆæ¯æ¥è‡ª ttl ä¸º 10S çš„é˜Ÿåˆ—: " + message);
        rabbitTemplate.convertAndSend("X", "XB", "æ¶ˆæ¯æ¥è‡ª ttl ä¸º 40S çš„é˜Ÿåˆ—: " + message);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      æ¶ˆæ¯æ¶ˆè´¹è€…

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.consumer;

import com.rabbitmq.client.Channel;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.amqp.core.Message;
import org.springframework.amqp.rabbit.annotation.RabbitListener;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.Date;

@Slf4j
@Component
public class DeadLetterQueueConsumer {
    @RabbitListener(queues = {"QD"})
    public void receiveD(Message message, Channel channel) {
        String msg = new String(message.getBody());
        log.info("å½“å‰æ—¶é—´ï¼š{},æ”¶åˆ°æ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¿¡æ¯{}", new Date().toString(), msg);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      @Configuration
public class MsgTtlQueueConfig {
    private static final String Y_DEAD_LETTER_EXCHANGE = "Y";
    private static final String QUEUE_C = "QC";
    private static final String X_EXCHANGE_QUEUE_C_ROUTING_KEY = "XC";
    private static final String Y_DEAD_QUEUE_D_ROUTING_KEY = "YD";

    @Bean("queueC")
    public Queue queueC() {
        HashMap<String, Object> params = new HashMap<>();
        params.put("x-dead-letter-exchange", Y_DEAD_LETTER_EXCHANGE);
        params.put("x-dead-letter-routing-key", Y_DEAD_QUEUE_D_ROUTING_KEY);
        return QueueBuilder.durable(QUEUE_C).withArguments(params).build();
    }

    @Bean
    public Binding queuecBindingX(@Qualifier("queueC") Queue queue, 
                                  @Qualifier("xExchange") DirectExchange exchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(queue).to(exchange).with(X_EXCHANGE_QUEUE_C_ROUTING_KEY);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      @Configuration
public class DelayedQueueConfig {
    public static final String DELAYED_QUEUE_NAME = "delayed.queue";
    public static final String DELAYED_EXCHANGE_NAME = "delayed.exchange";
    public static final String DELAYED_ROUTING_KEY = "delayed.routingkey";

    @Bean
    public Queue delayedQueue() {
        return new Queue(DELAYED_QUEUE_NAME);
    }

    @Bean
    public CustomExchange delayedExchange() {
        Map<String, Object> args = new HashMap<>();
        args.put("x-delayed-type", "direct");
        /**
         * å»¶è¿Ÿäº¤æ¢æœºåç§°
         * äº¤æ¢æœºç±»å‹
         * æŒä¹…åŒ–
         * è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ é™¤
         */
        return new CustomExchange(DELAYED_EXCHANGE_NAME, "x-delayed-message", true, false, args);
    }

    @Bean
    public Binding bindingDelayedQueue(@Qualifier("delayedQueue") Queue queue,
                                       @Qualifier("delayedExchange") CustomExchange delayedExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(queue).to(delayedExchange).with(DELAYED_ROUTING_KEY).noargs();
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      @Configuration
public class ConfirmConfig {
    public static final String CONFIRM_EXCHANGE_NAME = "confirm.exchange";
    public static final String CONFIRM_QUEUE_NAME = "confirm.queue";

    @Bean("confirmExchange")
    public DirectExchange confirmExchange() {
        return new DirectExchange(CONFIRM_EXCHANGE_NAME);
    }

    @Bean("confirmQueue")
    public Queue confirmQueue() {
        return QueueBuilder.durable(CONFIRM_QUEUE_NAME).build();
    }

    @Bean
    public Binding queueBinding(@Qualifier("confirmQueue") Queue queue,
                                @Qualifier("confirmExchange") DirectExchange exchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(queue).to(exchange).with("key1");
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      package com.example.rabbitmq.config;

import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.amqp.rabbit.connection.CorrelationData;
import org.springframework.amqp.rabbit.core.RabbitTemplate;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import javax.annotation.PostConstruct;

@Slf4j
@Component
public class MyCallBack implements RabbitTemplate.ConfirmCallback {
    /**
     * æ³¨æ„éœ€è¦è®¾ç½® RabbitTemplate.ConfirmCallback çš„å€¼
     */
    @Autowired
    private RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate;

    @PostConstruct
    public void init() {
        rabbitTemplate.setConfirmCallback(this);
    }

    @Override
    public void confirm(CorrelationData correlationData, boolean ack, String cause) {
        String id = correlationData != null ? correlationData.getId() : "";
        if (ack) {
            log.info("äº¤æ¢æœºå·²ç»æ”¶åˆ° id ä¸º:{}çš„æ¶ˆæ¯", id);
        } else {
            log.info("äº¤æ¢æœºè¿˜æœªæ”¶åˆ° id ä¸º:{}æ¶ˆæ¯,ç”±äºåŸå› :{}", id, cause);
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      @RestController
@RequestMapping("/confirm")
@Slf4j
public class ProduceController {
    public static final String CONFIRM_EXCHANGE_NAME = "confirm.exchange";
    @Autowired
    private RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate;

    @GetMapping("sendMessage/{message}")
    public void sendMessage(@PathVariable String message) {
        //æŒ‡å®šæ¶ˆæ¯ id ä¸º 1
        CorrelationData correlationData1 = new CorrelationData("1");
        String routingKey = "key1";

        rabbitTemplate.convertAndSend(CONFIRM_EXCHANGE_NAME, routingKey, message + routingKey, correlationData1);
        CorrelationData correlationData2 = new CorrelationData("2");
        routingKey = "key2";

        rabbitTemplate.convertAndSend(CONFIRM_EXCHANGE_NAME, routingKey, message + routingKey, correlationData2);
        log.info("å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯å†…å®¹:{}", message);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      @Slf4j
@Component
public class MessageProducer implements RabbitTemplate.ConfirmCallback,
RabbitTemplate.ReturnCallback {
    @Autowired
    private RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate;

    //rabbitTemplate æ³¨å…¥ä¹‹åå°±è®¾ç½®è¯¥å€¼
    @PostConstruct
    private void init() {
        rabbitTemplate.setConfirmCallback(this);
        /**
         * trueï¼š
         * äº¤æ¢æœºæ— æ³•å°†æ¶ˆæ¯è¿›è¡Œè·¯ç”±æ—¶ï¼Œä¼šå°†è¯¥æ¶ˆæ¯è¿”å›ç»™ç”Ÿäº§è€…
         * falseï¼š
         * å¦‚æœå‘ç°æ¶ˆæ¯æ— æ³•è¿›è¡Œè·¯ç”±ï¼Œåˆ™ç›´æ¥ä¸¢å¼ƒ
         */
        rabbitTemplate.setMandatory(true);
        //è®¾ç½®å›é€€æ¶ˆæ¯äº¤ç»™è°å¤„ç†
        rabbitTemplate.setReturnCallback(this);
    }

    @GetMapping("sendMessage")
    public void sendMessage(String message) {
        //è®©æ¶ˆæ¯ç»‘å®šä¸€ä¸ª id å€¼
        CorrelationData correlationData1 = new CorrelationData(UUID.randomUUID().toString());
        rabbitTemplate.convertAndSend("confirm.exchange", "key1", message + "key1", correlationData1)
        ;
        log.info("å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯ id ä¸º:{}å†…å®¹ä¸º{}", correlationData1.getId(), message + "key1");
        CorrelationData correlationData2 = new CorrelationData(UUID.randomUUID().toString());

        rabbitTemplate.convertAndSend("confirm.exchange", "key2", message + "key2", correlationData2)
        ;
        log.info("å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯ id ä¸º:{}å†…å®¹ä¸º{}", correlationData2.getId(), message + "key2");
    }

    @Override
    public void confirm(CorrelationData correlationData, boolean ack, String cause) {
        String id = correlationData != null ? correlationData.getId() : "";
        if (ack) {
            log.info("äº¤æ¢æœºæ”¶åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯ç¡®è®¤æˆåŠŸ, id:{}", id);
        } else {
            log.error("æ¶ˆæ¯ id:{}æœªæˆåŠŸæŠ•é€’åˆ°äº¤æ¢æœº,åŸå› æ˜¯:{}", id, cause);
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void returnedMessage(Message message, int replyCode, String replyText, String
            exchange, String routingKey) {
        log.info("æ¶ˆæ¯:{}è¢«æœåŠ¡å™¨é€€å›ï¼Œé€€å›åŸå› :{}, äº¤æ¢æœºæ˜¯:{}, è·¯ç”± key:{}",
                new String(message.getBody()), replyText, exchange, routingKey);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      @Configuration
public class ConfirmConfig {
    public static final String CONFIRM_EXCHANGE_NAME = "confirm.exchange";
    public static final String CONFIRM_QUEUE_NAME = "confirm.queue";
    public static final String BACKUP_EXCHANGE_NAME = "backup.exchange";
    public static final String BACKUP_QUEUE_NAME = "backup.queue";
    public static final String WARNING_QUEUE_NAME = "warning.queue";

    // å£°æ˜ç¡®è®¤é˜Ÿåˆ—
    @Bean("confirmQueue")
    public Queue confirmQueue() {
        return QueueBuilder.durable(CONFIRM_QUEUE_NAME).build();
    }

    //å£°æ˜ç¡®è®¤é˜Ÿåˆ—ç»‘å®šå…³ç³»
    @Bean
    public Binding queueBinding(@Qualifier("confirmQueue") Queue queue,
                                @Qualifier("confirmExchange") DirectExchange exchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(queue).to(exchange).with("key1");
    }

    //å£°æ˜å¤‡ä»½ Exchange
    @Bean("backupExchange")
    public FanoutExchange backupExchange() {
        return new FanoutExchange(BACKUP_EXCHANGE_NAME);
    }

    //å£°æ˜ç¡®è®¤ Exchange äº¤æ¢æœºçš„å¤‡ä»½äº¤æ¢æœº
    @Bean("confirmExchange")
    public DirectExchange confirmExchange() {
        ExchangeBuilder exchangeBuilder =
                ExchangeBuilder.directExchange(CONFIRM_EXCHANGE_NAME)
                        .durable(true)
                        //è®¾ç½®è¯¥äº¤æ¢æœºçš„å¤‡ä»½äº¤æ¢æœº
                        .withArgument("alternate-exchange", BACKUP_EXCHANGE_NAME);
        return (DirectExchange) exchangeBuilder.build();
    }

    // å£°æ˜è­¦å‘Šé˜Ÿåˆ—
    @Bean("warningQueue")
    public Queue warningQueue() {
        return QueueBuilder.durable(WARNING_QUEUE_NAME).build();
    }

    // å£°æ˜æŠ¥è­¦é˜Ÿåˆ—ç»‘å®šå…³ç³»
    @Bean
    public Binding warningBinding(@Qualifier("warningQueue") Queue queue,
                                  @Qualifier("backupExchange") FanoutExchange
                                          backupExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(queue).to(backupExchange);
    }

    // å£°æ˜å¤‡ä»½é˜Ÿåˆ—
    @Bean("backQueue")
    public Queue backQueue() {
        return QueueBuilder.durable(BACKUP_QUEUE_NAME).build();
    }

    // å£°æ˜å¤‡ä»½é˜Ÿåˆ—ç»‘å®šå…³ç³»
    @Bean
    public Binding backupBinding(@Qualifier("backQueue") Queue queue,
                                 @Qualifier("backupExchange") FanoutExchange backupExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(queue).to(backupExchange);
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      public class Producer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "hello";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        try (Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();) {
            //ç»™æ¶ˆæ¯èµ‹äºˆä¸€ä¸ª priority å±æ€§
            AMQP.BasicProperties properties = new
                    AMQP.BasicProperties().builder().priority(5).build();
            for (int i = 1; i < 11; i++) {
                String message = "info" + i;
                if (i == 5) {
                    channel.basicPublish("", QUEUE_NAME, properties, message.getBytes());
                } else {
                    channel.basicPublish("", QUEUE_NAME, null, message.getBytes());
                }
                System.out.println("å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯å®Œæˆ:" + message);
            }
        }
    }
}

                                                                                                                                      public class Consumer {
    private static final String QUEUE_NAME = "hello";

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Channel channel = RabbitConnectUtil.getChannel();
        //è®¾ç½®é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„æœ€å¤§ä¼˜å…ˆçº§ æœ€å¤§å¯ä»¥è®¾ç½®åˆ° 255 å®˜ç½‘æ¨è 1-10 å¦‚æœè®¾ç½®å¤ªé«˜æ¯”è¾ƒåƒå†…å­˜å’Œ CPU

        params.put("x-max-priority", 10);
        channel.queueDeclare(QUEUE_NAME, true, false, false, params);
        System.out.println("æ¶ˆè´¹è€…å¯åŠ¨ç­‰å¾…æ¶ˆè´¹......");
        DeliverCallback deliverCallback = (consumerTag, delivery) -> {
            String receivedMessage = new String(delivery.getBody());
            System.out.println("æ¥æ”¶åˆ°æ¶ˆæ¯:" + receivedMessage);
        };
        channel.basicConsume(QUEUE_NAME, true, deliverCallback, (consumerTag) -> {
            System.out.println("æ¶ˆè´¹è€…æ— æ³•æ¶ˆè´¹æ¶ˆæ¯æ—¶è°ƒç”¨ï¼Œå¦‚é˜Ÿåˆ—è¢«åˆ é™¤");
        });
    }
}
